      $(document).ready(function(){
	$('#search-in-start').change(function(){$('#query-start').attr("name",$(this).val());});
	$('#search-term-start input.submit-search').on("click",function(){if($('input#query-start').val()=='Search Juno...'){window.location.replace('/search/'); return false;};});
	$("#search-term-start").submit(function(){var inputValue=$("#query-start").val();$("#query-start").val($.trim(inputValue));});
	$("#search-term").submit(function(){var inputValue=$("#query").val();$("#query").val($.trim(inputValue));});
});

  <script>
   $(document).ready(function() {
	$.getJSON('/api/1.2/widget/getNavigationJson', function( data ) {
		$('#nav li').each(function(){
			if(data[$(this).attr('id')] !== undefined)
				$(data[$(this).attr('id')]).appendTo($(this));
			$(this).mouseout(function(){drop_down_hide_delay_nav();}).mouseover(function(){drop_down_show_nav($(this).attr('id'));});
		});
		if(selectedNav)do_drop_down_show_nav(selectedNav);
	});
});
  </script>

  <script>
   show_nmd = function(){
	var promotionDialogNmd = $('#dialog-nmd');
	if(promotionDialogNmd.length &gt; 0){
		promotionDialogNmd.dialog({
			width: 500,
	        height: 500,
	        modal: true,
	        autoOpen: true,
	        draggable: false,
	        resizable: false,
	        show: 'fade',
	        hide: 'fade',
	        title: ''
	    });
		$('#btn-nmd-continue-shopping').on('click', function () { $('#dialog-nmd').dialog('close'); });
		$('#btn-nmd-goto').on('click', function () { 
			ga('send', 'event', 'DigitalMove', 'Click to JD');
			if(window.location.href.indexOf('juno.co.uk/wishlist') &gt; -1)
				window.location.href = 'http://www.junodownload.com/wishlist/';
			else
				window.location.href = 'http://www.junodownload.com/';
		});
	}
}
  </script>
